    5610             : #ifdef MOZ_X11
    5611             : // For long-lived popup windows that don't really take focus themselves but
    5612             : // may have elements that accept keyboard input when the parent window is
    5613             : // active, focus is handled specially.  These windows include noautohide
    5614             : // panels.  (This special handling is not necessary for temporary popups where
    5615             : // the keyboard is grabbed.)
    5616             : //
    5617             : // Mousing over or clicking on these windows should not cause them to steal
    5618             : // focus from their parent windows, so, the input field of WM_HINTS is set to
    5619             : // False to request that the window manager not set the input focus to this
    5620             : // window.  http://tronche.com/gui/x/icccm/sec-4.html#s-4.1.7
    5621             : //
    5622             : // However, these windows can still receive WM_TAKE_FOCUS messages from the
    5623             : // window manager, so they can still detect when the user has indicated that
    5624             : // they wish to direct keyboard input at these windows.  When the window
    5625             : // manager offers focus to these windows (after a mouse over or click, for
    5626             : // example), a request to make the parent window active is issued.  When the
    5627             : // parent window becomes active, keyboard events will be received.
    5628             :
